2026-03-15T16:42:45.4632764Z     {
2026-03-15T16:42:45.4632949Z         static bool s_prev[256] = {};

2026-03-15T16:42:45.4633569Z         bool just = curr && !s_prev[vk];

2026-03-15T16:42:45.4634403Z         return just;

2026-03-15T16:42:45.4765461Z         ++g_logFrame;
2026-03-15T16:42:45.4765802Z     
2026-03-15T16:42:45.4766213Z         CPlayerPed* player = CWorld::Players[0].m_pPed;
2026-03-15T16:42:45.4766749Z         if (!player) return;

2026-03-15T16:43:44.2024336Z copilot: Now let me understand the full picture based on all the code I've read and the problem statement:
2026-03-15T16:43:44.2025240Z 
2026-03-15T16:43:44.2025630Z **Current Issues:**
2026-03-15T16:43:44.2027076Z 1. **Recruit doesn't follow player in cars as passenger** - When player is in a vehicle, the recruit stays on foot and does not try to enter the same vehicle as passenger
2026-03-15T16:43:44.2028986Z 2. **Respect stat manipulation** - The user says we shouldn't need to manipulate respect as it's part of game progression
2026-03-15T16:43:44.2030052Z 3. **Driving mode issues:**
2026-03-15T16:43:44.2030518Z    - CIVICO_D: Problems following closely
2026-03-15T16:43:44.2031077Z    - CIVICO_E: Better but doesn't make turns
2026-03-15T16:43:44.2031729Z    - DIRETO: Recruit bumps into player's car or passes in front
2026-03-15T16:43:44.2044895Z 
2026-03-15T16:43:44.2044914Z 
2026-03-15T16:43:44.2045691Z 4. **New driving modes needed** and the recruit needs to recognize when the player is in a vehicle and follow appropriately on the road
2026-03-15T16:43:44.2046598Z 
2026-03-15T16:43:44.2057688Z The core issue is that the recruit needs to detect when the player is driving and either enter the vehicle as a driver or follow on foot while staying on the road, rather than just standing still or wandering off. So the recruit needs to automatically enter the player's vehicle as a passenger when the player gets in while on foot—that's the core vanilla GTA SA behavior that's missing. Beyond that, there are issues with the CIVICO driving modes where CIVICO_D follows too closely and CIVICO_E won't turn, while DIRETO mode either bumps into or passes the player's car. I should check the copilot log to see what was already discovered about these driving behaviors. Looking at the available car missions in GTA SA, I can see there are several options that might work better for the recruit following behavior—APPROACHPLAYER_CLOSE for tight following, FOLLOWCAR_FARAWAY for distance-based following, and ESCORT_REAR variants for road-aware movement. The key is picking missions that handle turns and obstacles naturally without the recruit getting stuck or losing the player. 2026-03-15T16:45:12.3443770Z     
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3444350Z     | | VS Code | Visual Studio |
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3444744Z     |---|---|---|
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3445352Z     | O que é | Editor de texto leve | IDE com compilador C++ |
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3446085Z     | Compila C++? | ❌ Não sozinho | ✅ Sim (MSVC incluído) |
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3446745Z     | O que precisas | — | **Este aqui** |
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3447168Z     
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3448338Z     **VS Code sozinho não compila C++.** Para compilar este mod precisas do **Visual Studio Community** (gratuito) com o workload `Desktop development with C++`.
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3449467Z     
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3450046Z     Podes ter os dois instalados ao mesmo tempo — não há conflito.

2026-03-15T16:45:12.3451550Z     ## O que é este ficheiro
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3451941Z     
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3453586Z     `grove_recruit_standalone.asi` é uma DLL renomeada que o GTA SA carrega automaticamente na inicialização (via ASI Loader). Substitui completamente o `grove_recruit_follow.cs` — não precisa de CLEO para funcionar.

2026-03-15T16:45:12.3464502Z     ## Caminho rápido (script automático)
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3465134Z     
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3465736Z     1. **Instale o Visual Studio Community 2022** se ainda não o fez:
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3466392Z        - Vai a https://visualstudio.microsoft.com/
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3467586Z        - Descarrega e instala o **Visual Studio Community**
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3468946Z        - Durante a instalação, selecciona o workload **"Desktop development with C++"**
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3469632Z     
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3470052Z     2. **Instale o Git** se ainda não o tem:
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3470746Z        - Vai a https://git-scm.com e instala com as opções padrão
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3471270Z     
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3471647Z     3. **Edita o `setup_and_build.bat`** num editor de texto:
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3472136Z        ```bat
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3472604Z        set GTA_SA_PATH=C:\Program Files (x86)\Rockstar Games\GTA San Andreas
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3473234Z        set PLUGIN_SDK_DIR=C:\dev\plugin-sdk
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3473689Z        ```
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3475003Z        Substitui pelo caminho real do teu GTA SA. O `PLUGIN_SDK_DIR` pode ficar em `C:\dev\plugin-sdk` (será criado automaticamente).
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3475904Z     
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3476283Z     4. **Clica duas vezes** no `setup_and_build.bat`
2026-03-15T16:45:12.3476793Z     <exited with exit code 0>

2026-03-15T16:45:48.2062139Z ### Issues to Fix:
2026-03-15T16:45:48.2062366Z 
2026-03-15T16:45:48.2063129Z 1. **Recruit doesn't follow player as passenger in car** - When player enters a vehicle, recruit should automatically enter as passenger (like vanilla gang members do). This is the KEY behavioral issue.
2026-03-15T16:45:48.2064205Z 
2026-03-15T16:45:48.2064304Z 2. **Driving modes**:
2026-03-15T16:45:48.2064679Z    - CIVICO_D: Still has issues following closely 
2026-03-15T16:45:48.2065349Z    - CIVICO_E: Better but doesn't make turns well
2026-03-15T16:45:48.2065982Z    - DIRETO: Bumps into player's car or passes in front
2026-03-15T16:45:48.2066389Z 
2026-03-15T16:45:48.2067019Z 3. **New driving modes** needed - The user wants to test CIVICO-style road-following but with car/pedestrian avoidance
2026-03-15T16:45:48.2067946Z    
2026-03-15T16:45:48.2077218Z Looking at the car mission constants in the code, I can see the different follow behaviors available - ESCORT_REAR for close following, APPROACHPLAYER variants for different distances, and FOLLOWCAR modes with their own distance variations. The key is figuring out which mission type will make the recruit stay with the player's vehicle properly. I should set aside the naming inconsistencies between the config comments and the actual mission IDs, and instead focus on understanding what each mission actually does. Looking at the eCarMission enum values, I can see the mission IDs map to specific behaviors—MISSION_34 handles following recorded paths, MISSION_43 and MISSION_44 handle approaching the player at different distances, and MISSION_52 onwards handle following cars at various ranges. There's a discrepancy between what the config.h comments claim and what the GetCarMissionName function actually returns—the config says CIVICO_D uses mission 43 which is "EscortRearFaraway," but the log shows 43 maps to "APPROACHPLAYER_FARAWAY" and 67 maps to "ESCORT_REAR_FARAWAY." I'll treat the GetCarMissionName function as the authoritative source since the config comment appears to be incorrect. I'm seeing the confusion now—the enum constant `MISSION_43` actually has an integer value of 67 in the plugin-sdk, which is why the comment notes "(=67)". So the naming is misleading: the enum is called `MISSION_43` but it represents mission type 67, which corresponds to `ESCORT_REAR_FARAWAY`, not the mission 43 that `CIVICO_D` currently uses (`APPROACHPLAYER_FARAWAY`). Looking at the includes in grove_recruit_config.h, I see it references eCarMission.h from the plugin-sdk, but I can't locate those files directly in the repository to verify what the actual enum values are.

So the recruit stops dead at 11.4m even though it should be following the road at that distance. The real problem is that when CLOSE behavior kicks in, it switches to direct chase mode toward the player instead of staying on roads, and the WRONG_DIR recovery check at distances under 30m prevents it from snapping back to proper road navigation. The transition from MISSION_43 to MISSION_31 happens at a specific distance threshold, but something in that handoff is breaking the pathfinding.

The better approach would be switching to FOLLOWCAR_CLOSE (53/MISSION_35) for close-range following since it's specifically designed for that behavior, rather than relying on ESCORT_REAR's direct positioning logic. 2026-03-15T17:02:12.9719568Z 
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9721797Z ESCORT_REAR calculates a specific geometric position behind the target and tries to reach it via the road graph, which can cause awkward direct-drive behavior when the recruit is already close or positioned to the side. FOLLOWCAR_CLOSE just mirrors the target's path naturally without forcing a specific position. The solution is to add a distance check in the driving AI that switches to FOLLOWCAR_CLOSE when the recruit gets within a short threshold like 25 meters, then reverts to the normal mission behavior once distance increases again.
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9724219Z 
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9727159Z Implementing this override in ProcessDrivingAI... I'm checking the mission constant definitions across the different libraries — MC_APPROACHPLAYER_FARAWAY maps to 43, but looking at the actual transitions in CIVICO_D from the logs, it only goes through 67 and 31, so I should simplify the condition to just check for MC_ESCORT_REAR.
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9729873Z 
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9731122Z The missing turns issue is probably a timing problem where the car doesn't brake early enough before curves, and the road-snap system at 3-second intervals might be missing the adjustment window.
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9732591Z 
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9735909Z The real issue is that AdaptiveSpeed reacts to heading misalignment after it's already happened, so by then the car has overshot the turn. I could predict upcoming turns by looking ahead at the next road node, or snap to the road more frequently. Reducing ROAD_SNAP_INTERVAL from 3 seconds to 1 second would let the car adjust heading more often before turns, but that risks triggering more INVALID_LINK issues since we already had to increase it from 300 frames to handle that problem.
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9739299Z 
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9741959Z Looking at how ApplyLaneAlignment clips the heading to the current link—that happens every frame, but the problem is it only considers the link the car is already on, not the one coming up. So on a straight section before a turn, the link still shows straight until the car reaches the actual turn point.
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9743674Z 
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9744907Z I think the better approach is a middle ground: bump ROAD_SNAP_INTERVAL to 90 frames for the CIVICO models where users report better handling but still miss turns, while keeping CIVICO_D at 180 frames since it has the close-range issue to manage.
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9746171Z 
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9748115Z But wait—the real culprit might be the WRONG_DIR logic itself. When the car misses a turn and the heading difference climbs toward 0.9-1.2, AdaptiveSpeed cuts the throttle but the car keeps going straight. Once it hits WRONG_DIR territory (>1.5), SetupDriveMode re-snaps the path, but only if the distance is over 30 meters. Below that threshold, nothing triggers and the car stays locked on the wrong direction.
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9749865Z 
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9750566Z So the fix is twofold: switch to close-range chase mode when distance drops below 25 meters in the affected models, and reduce the snap interval to catch turns faster.
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9751343Z 
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9753177Z For the WRONG_DIR issue at close range specifically—calling JoinCarWithRoadSystem when the car is nearby is actually dangerous because it can snap to a road node pointing the wrong way. The previous session found that disabling this call under 30 meters prevented those bad snaps, but now the car just gets stuck in WRONG_DIR until something else corrects it.
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9755519Z 
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9757179Z A better approach would be to switch to a gentler follow mode that keeps the car close to the player without the aggressive road snapping, maintain low speed, and let the state machine recover naturally. But I'm realizing that even this gentler mode might force the car to follow the player's direction rather than the road's, which could create its own problems.
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9759269Z 
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9761268Z For motorcycles specifically, there's an added complication—the player's motorcycle has an invalid link ID, so the recruit can't use road-graph targeting at all. The position-based follow mode might actually work better here since it doesn't rely on road data.
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9762659Z 
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9765563Z Let me outline the concrete fixes I need to implement for this close-range chase-mode issue. When the recruit is at close range in ESCORT_REAR mode, it's not just the WRONG_DIR case that causes problems—the normal escort behavior itself tries to position exactly behind the player, which can cause off-road steering on curves. So I should consolidate both issues into a single close-range override that switches to MC_FOLLOWCAR_CLOSE instead, and reduce the road snap interval to help track turns more responsively.
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9768102Z 
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9769286Z I also want to add a soft recovery for WRONG_DIR at close range—instead of aggressive intervention, just switching to MC_FOLLOWCAR_CLOSE will help the state machine transition to something more stable.
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9770194Z 
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9770392Z Defining the constants... Writing the close-range recovery logic...
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9770710Z 
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9771919Z I'm also thinking about tuning the road snap interval down to 90 frames for faster response, and I'm noticing that the turn-handling issues are probably most apparent in CIVICO_E mode, which uses a different mission type that the user mentioned performs better.
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9773121Z 
2026-03-15T17:02:12.9776881Z Looking at the speed calculations, when the heading delta is around 1.0, the adaptive speed multiplier drops to about 0.71, so the car should already be slowing down significantly for curves. But it seems like even at that reduced speed of 71% base speed, it's still missing turns at 77 km/h, which suggests the speed reduction might not be aggressive enough or the turn detection itself needs adjustment. should be straightforward—just tweaking the curve speed reduction slightly more aggressive, reducing how often the car recalculates its path, and adding a close-range override so it switches to tighter following behavior when near the player. I'll also make sure the passenger auto-enter feature gets included in this batch of changes.

2026-03-15T17:14:49.9888646Z ## O que foi feito
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9888866Z 
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9889117Z ### 1. **Auto-entrada no carro como passageiro** (comportamento vanilla restaurado)
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9890034Z - `ProcessOnFoot` detecta a transição `!bInVehicle → bInVehicle` no jogador
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9890915Z - Emite `CTaskComplexEnterCarAsPassenger` para o recruta entrar no mesmo carro
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9891913Z - Restrito a carros (`subClass=0`) e motas (`subClass=1`) com lugares livres (`m_nNumPassengers < m_nMaxPassengers`) e distância ≤60m
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9892921Z - Suprime `TellGroupFollowWithRespect` enquanto o jogador está em veículo (evita override da task)
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9894322Z - `g_enterCarAsPassenger=true` → `ProcessEnterCar` transita para **RIDING** em vez de DRIVING
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9895000Z 
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9895216Z ### 2. **Estado RIDING** (recruta como passageiro)
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9896148Z - `ProcessRiding` per-frame: deteta saída do jogador → emite `CTaskComplexLeaveCar` → volta a `ON_FOOT`
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9896772Z - Reset em `DismissRecruit`
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9896934Z 
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9897119Z ### 3. **Fix "chase mode" ao perto** (problema principal do utilizador)
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9897993Z - Causa: `MC_ESCORT_REAR (31)` tenta posicionar-se geometricamente-exato atrás do jogador, saindo da estrada quando próximo
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9899357Z - Fix: a `CLOSE_RANGE_SWITCH_DIST = 22m`, `ProcessDrivingAI` substitui silenciosamente mission=31 por `MC_FOLLOWCAR_CLOSE (53)` que segue o trajeto sem forçar posição
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9900458Z - **WRONG_DIR soft recovery** a <30m: muda mission para `MC_FOLLOWCAR_CLOSE` sem `JoinCarWithRoadSystem` (evita o re-snap errado)
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9901055Z 
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9901180Z ### 4. **Fix DIRETO** (batia/passava pelo jogador)
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9901704Z - Mudou `PLOUGH_THROUGH` → `STOP_FOR_CARS_IGNORE_LIGHTS`
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9902423Z - Destino = posição do jogador - **10m no heading do jogador** (para atrás), calculado via `GetPlayerHeading()` helper
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9902946Z 
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9903054Z ### 5. **Novos modos CIVICO_F e CIVICO_G**
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9903673Z - **CIVICO_F**: `MC_ESCORT_REAR_FARAWAY(67)` + `AVOID_CARS` — road-following evitando tráfego
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9904596Z - **CIVICO_G**: `MC_FOLLOWCAR_CLOSE(53)` + `AVOID_CARS` — seguimento próximo com desvio de obstáculos
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9905086Z 
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9905182Z ### 6. **Melhor tracking de curvas**
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9905730Z - `ROAD_SNAP_INTERVAL`: 180→**90 frames** (3s→1.5s) — mais frequente para não errar curvas
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9906421Z - `CURVE_SPEED_REDUCTION`: 0.5→**0.6** — travagem mais agressiva nas curvas
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9906840Z 
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9907002Z ### 7. **Remoção do boost de STAT_RESPECT**
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9907853Z - `MakeThisPedJoinOurGroup` chamado sem boost temporário — o fallback `AddFollower+EnsureBeInGroup` garante o follow mesmo com respeito 0
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9908515Z 
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9908607Z ### 8. **Aliases MC_ no config.h**
2026-03-15T17:14:49.9909343Z - Nomes legíveis da gta-reversed mapeados para os enums do plugin-sdk (ex: `MC_ESCORT_REAR_FARAWAY = MISSION_43 // int=67`)

2026-03-15T17:15:13.7647780Z Recruited gang member did not follow the player into vehicles (vanilla GTA SA behavior). Close-range driving triggered an off-road "chase mode" due to `MC_ESCORT_REAR(31)` forcing geometric positioning. `DIRETO` mode drove through the player's car. Two new avoidance-capable drive modes added.
2026-03-15T17:15:13.7649962Z 
2026-03-15T17:15:13.7650139Z ## Auto-enter car as passenger
2026-03-15T17:15:13.7651753Z - `ProcessOnFoot` detects `!bInVehicle → bInVehicle` transition on player; issues `CTaskComplexEnterCarAsPassenger` to recruit
2026-03-15T17:15:13.7653131Z - Only for `subClass ≤ 1` (cars/motos) with free seats; recruit must be within 60 m
2026-03-15T17:15:13.7654458Z - `TellGroupFollowWithRespect` suppressed while player is in vehicle to avoid overriding the passenger task
2026-03-15T17:15:13.7656034Z - `g_enterCarAsPassenger` flag routes `ENTER_CAR → RIDING` (new `ModState::RIDING=5`) instead of `DRIVING`
2026-03-15T17:15:13.7657359Z - `ProcessRiding` per-frame: detects player exit → issues `CTaskComplexLeaveCar` → back to `ON_FOOT`
2026-03-15T17:15:13.7657999Z 
2026-03-15T17:15:13.7658144Z ## Close-range "chase mode" fix
2026-03-15T17:15:13.7658936Z `MC_ESCORT_REAR(31)` geometrically anchors the recruit behind the player and pulls it off the road at short range. Fix:
2026-03-15T17:15:13.7660363Z - At `dist < 22 m` (`CLOSE_RANGE_SWITCH_DIST`), `ProcessDrivingAI` silently overrides `mission=31` → `MC_FOLLOWCAR_CLOSE(53)` each frame
2026-03-15T17:15:13.7662093Z - `WRONG_DIR` at `dist ≤ 30 m`: soft recovery sets `MC_FOLLOWCAR_CLOSE` **without** `JoinCarWithRoadSystem` (that call caused 38 s bad-navigation episodes when issued close-up)
2026-03-15T17:15:13.7663043Z 
2026-03-15T17:15:13.7663153Z ## DIRETO fix
2026-03-15T17:15:13.7663580Z - `PLOUGH_THROUGH` → `STOP_FOR_CARS_IGNORE_LIGHTS`
2026-03-15T17:15:13.7664726Z - Destination offset **10 m behind** player heading via new `GetPlayerHeading()` helper (deduplicates two identical inline calculations)
2026-03-15T17:15:13.7665731Z ```cpp
2026-03-15T17:15:13.7666314Z float playerHeading = GetPlayerHeading(player);           // car heading or ped rotation
2026-03-15T17:15:13.7667209Z CVector dest = player->GetPosition() - pFwd * DIRETO_FOLLOW_OFFSET;
2026-03-15T17:15:13.7667740Z ```
2026-03-15T17:15:13.7667883Z
